* FIXes:
********
The easy fix step-by-step:
Windows Update Blocker (WUB) for Windows 10:
http://www.sordum.org/9470/
File:
http://www.sordum.org/files/download/windows-update-blocker/Wub.zip
Screen shot:
http://www.sordum.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/windos_update_blocker_blocked.png
A. Use an unZIPping/unARChiving/unRARing tool [free(ware)]
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#ZIP
to open "Wub.zip" archive and extract "Wub.exe" + "Wub.ini" into the same dedicated/empty directory/folder: I have used
C:\TOOLS_10 in this example.
B. Open Explorer/similar/replacement -> right-click "Wub.exe" -> Run as Administrator -> (1) check "Disable Updates" box ->
(2) check "Protect Services Settings" box -> (3) click "Apply Now" -> close/exit WUB.
http://www.sordum.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/windos_update_blocker_blocked.png
C. Add this entry to your HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE (HKLM) machine/system wide/all users registry "Run" subkey (example):
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Run]
"WUB"="\"C:\\TOOLS_10\\WUB.EXE\" /D /P"
;
------End cut & paste here------
In this example WUB.EXE is located in the C:\TOOLS_10 folder.
D. OR:
Create a new task to run Windows Update Blocker (WUB) periodically scheduled (say once a day) in the background using
Task Scheduler (TaskSchd.msc) located in the %WinDir%\SYSTEM32 folder [where %WinDir% = usually C:\WINDOWS]:
http://www.windowscentral.com/how-create-automated-task-using-task-scheduler-windows-10/
Start -> Run... [hold WinKey + press R] -> type
TaskSchd.msc
-> press Enter -> right-click "Task Scheduler Library" folder -> New Folder -> type folder name (Tasks_10 in this example)
-> Action top menu option -> Create Basic Task -> Create Basic Task Wizard -> type new task name in Name field
(WUB_Run_Daily in this example) -> Next button -> check Daily box -> Next button -> check Start a program box ->
Program/script field -> Browse button -> go to (I have used C:\TOOLS_10 folder in this example)
C:\TOOLS_10\WUB.EXE
-> Add arguments (optional) box -> type
/D /P
-> Finish button.
Tools similar to Windows Update Blocker (WUB) [free(ware)]:
http://www.majorgeeks.com/mg/sortdate/windows_update.html
Wu10Man for Windows 10 stops Windows Updates (WU) by tweaking Registry (Group Policy), disabling services + blocking URLs:
http://weredev.com/developer/wu10man/
http://github.com/WereDev/Wu10Man/
Download:
http://github.com/WereDev/Wu10Man/releases/latest/
Requires Microsoft .Net Framework Redistributable (NFR) 4.7.2/newer:
http://www.mdgx.com/add.htm#NFR
E. Reboot.

* OPTIONAL Steps + Explanation:
*******************************
All steps below are optional if you wish to do this step-by-step by hand/manually, or/and if you'd like to learn about the
complicated process and the tremendous length Microsoft went to in order to forbid Windows 10 users from disabling/stopping
Windows Updates. Wow!
WUB Brief Explanation:
**********************
Windows Update Blocker (WUB) disables + protects (by changing ownership rights, access, permissions, modyfing, renaming +/-
overwriting them) these Windows Updates (WU) interconnected/interdependent/related services:
- Backup Scan = runs by default upon every (re)boot + periodically in the background -> %systemroot%\system32\usoclient.exe
- Schedule Scan = runs by default upon every (re)boot + periodically in the background -> %systemroot%\system32\usoclient.exe
- Schedule Scan Static Task = runs by default upon every (re)boot + periodically in the background -> %systemroot%\system32\usoclient.exe
- UpdateModelTask = runs by default upon every (re)boot + periodically in the background -> %systemroot%\system32\usoclient.exe
- USO_UxBroker = runs by default upon every (re)boot + periodically in the background -> %systemroot%\system32\MusNotification.exe
found in this scheduled Tasks folder:
%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\UpdateOrchestrator
and also turns off, disables + protects (by changing ownership rights, modyfing, renaming +/- overwriting them) these
Windows Updates (WU) interconnected/interdependent/related services -> see respective Registry + BATch files below:
- DoSvc [Delivery Optimization service]
- UsoSvc [Update Orchestrator service]
- WaaSMedicSvc [Windows Update Medic service]
http://appuals.com/what-is-waasmedic-and-how-to-disable-it-and-fix-it/
- wuauserv [Windows Update (Automatic Updates) service]
WUB also stops temporarily this related service:
- BITS [Background Intelligent Transfer service]
WUB adds these REG_DWORD (DWORD) 32-bit values to the registry for all 4 Windows Updates (WU) interconnected/interdependent/related
services listed above:
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\DoSvc]
"WubLock"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\UsoSvc]
"WubLock"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WaaSMedicSvc]
"WubLock"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\wuauserv]
"WubLock"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\UsoSvc]
"WubLock"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\DoSvc]
"WubLock"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WaaSMedicSvc]
"WubLock"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\wuauserv]
"WubLock"=dword:1
;
------End cut & paste here------
Original (unmodified) Windows 10 Windows Updates (WU) built-in scheduled tasks are found in these TrustedInstaller
(%WinDir%\servicing\TrustedInstaller.exe = %WinDir% is usually C:\WINDOWS), Microsoft built-in user account [special "VIP" type
user created by Microsoft as "master overseer"] protected folders, which are disabled/forbidden/locked/unavailable to any
(other) user, even to the computer owner/main/only user, even with Admin(istrator)/Sysadmin/SYSTEM level:
C:\WINDOWS\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\UpdateOrchestrator :
Backup Scan
Maintenance Install
Reboot_AC Reboot_Battery
Schedule Scan
Schedule Scan Static Task
UpdateModelTask
USO_UxBroker
C:\WINDOWS\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\WaaSMedic :
PerformRemediation
C:\WINDOWS\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\WindowsUpdate :
Scheduled Start
sihpostreboot
To be allowed to access all these scheduled tasks one must take ownership + grant themselves Admin privileges to the respective
folders + files from a DOS console (command prompt) -> right-click CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE -> Run as Administrator -> run these
commands -> press Enter after each line:
TAKEOWN.EXE /f "%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks" /r /d y
ICACLS.EXE "%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks" /grant:r %UserName%:F /t /c /q
iCACLS.exe:
http://www.ss64.com/nt/icacls.html
TAKEOWN.exe:
http://www.ss64.com/nt/takeown.html
FYI:
NTFS Permissions Tools (NPT) 32-bit + 64-bit display/modify/add/delete NTFS ACLs file system security options/owner:
http://www.majorgeeks.com/files/details/ntfs_permissions_tools.html
Download:
http://www.softpedia.com/get/Internet/Servers/Server-Tools/NTFS-Permissions-Tools.shtml#download
Then rename all the Tasks subfolders listed above to anything else (example) from a DOS console (command prompt) ->
right-click CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE -> Run as Administrator -> run these commands -> press Enter after each line:
REN %WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\UpdateOrchestrator UpdateOrchestrator_OLD
REN %WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\WaaSMedic WaaSMedic_OLD
REN %WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\WindowsUpdate WindowsUpdate_OLD
OR run Task Scheduler MMC snap-in:
MMC.EXE /S taskschd.msc
and disable all the tasks listed above -> right-click on each one of them 1 at a time -> click Disable each time.
FYI:
TrustedInstaller (%WinDir%\servicing\TrustedInstaller.exe = %WinDir% is usually C:\WINDOWS) is Windows NTx
[Vista/2008/7/8/8.1/2012/10/2016/2019/11/2022/newer] Microsoft built-in user account [special "VIP" type user created by
Microsoft as "master overseer"] with privileged, above-admin, system-wide rights which performs
automatic/unattended/forced/behind-your-back/without-your-consent operations, for example: downloads, updates,
installs/uninstalls, closes/executes/(re)starts/(re)schedules dynamic link libraries (DLLs)/executables/services/tasks/scripts,
modifies the Registry, creates/copies/renames/modifies/moves/deletes files/folders, modifies/takes over files/folders
ownership/permissions/attributes, reboots/restarts/shuts down Windows.
See "* Everything about TrustedInstaller: info, guides, fixes, workarounds + tweaks:" in WINDOWS7.TXT (included):
http://www.mdgx.com/7.php
http://www.mdgx.com/WINDOWS7.TXT
How to stop Windows Updates (WU) [wuauserv] service + TrustedInstaller [TrustedInstaller.exe] process:
1. Run... [hold WinKey + press R] -> type:
services.msc
-> press Enter -> double-click Windows Updates (WU) service -> Stop button -> wait for service to stop -> OK button ->
immediately double-click Windows Updates (WU) again -> General tab -> Startup type: -> select Manual -> Recovery tab ->
"First Failure:", "Second Failure:" + "Subsequent Failures:" -> select Take No Action for all 3 types of Failure -> OK button.
2. Hold Ctrl + Shift + press Esc -> Task Manager (TaskMgr.exe) -> Processes tab -> right-click TrustedInstaller.exe -> End task
-> End process button -> close Task Manager.
All attempts to stop and/or disable these services/executables/processes/scheduled tasks manually by using:
Services MMC snap-in (%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Services.msc)
Task Scheduler MMC snap-in (%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\TaskSchd.msc)
RegEdit (%WinDir%\REGEDIT.EXE)
built-in DOS command console tools (examples): REG.EXE, NET.EXE, SC.EXE, TASKKILL.EXE, etc,
are usually unsuccessful on their own and/or by themselves, or when performed as any user other than TrustedInstaller, because
Windows restarts/reschedules/restores them afterwards almost immediately, or after a certain amount of time preset in the
built-in scheduled tasks/services/registry settings/run commands, and/or after the 1st reboot.
That's why multiple consecutive steps are required to be performed in a certain order for this to succeed.
1st Things 1st:
***************
BACKUP YOUR REGISTRY BEFORE MAKING ANY CHANGES! -> See "BACKUP/EXPORT + RESTORE/IMPORT REGISTRY/REGISTRY KEY(S)" in
WINDOWS7.TXT (included):
http://www.mdgx.com/7.php
http://www.mdgx.com/WINDOWS7.TXT
Step 1:
*******
Delay/Defer/Pause/Postpone Windows Update service (WuauServ) by running BATch file below:
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text BATch (.bat) or CoMmanD (.cmd) script file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the BAT (.bat) or CMD (.cmd) extension.
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created BATch/CoMmanD file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Wait for completion.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
@ECHO OFF
IF NOT "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" GOTO END
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\WindowsUpdateSysprepInProgress" /f
WMIC.EXE service wuauserv call StopService
RUNDLL32.EXE wuaueng.dll,GeneralizeForImaging
:END
EXIT
------End cut & paste here------
Step 2:
*******
Delay/Defer/Pause/Postpone Windows Update (WU) by running Registry file below:
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\WindowsSelfHost\UI\Visibility
"HideInsiderPage"=dword:1

[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\WindowsUpdate\UX]
"IsConvergedUpdateStackEnabled"=dword:0

[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\WindowsUpdate\UX\Settings]
"AllowAutoWindowsUpdateDownloadOverMeteredNetwork"=dword:0
"BranchReadinessLevel"=dword:10
"ConfigureDeadlineForFeatureUpdates"=dword:1e
"ConfigureDeadlineForQualityUpdates"=dword:1e
"DeferFeatureUpdates"=dword:1
"DeferFeatureUpdatesPeriodInDays"=dword:16d
"DeferQualityUpdatesPeriodInDays"=dword:16d
"DeferQualityUpdates"=dword:1
"DeferQualityUpdatesPeriodInDays"=dword:1e
"DeferUpgrade"=dword:1
"DeferUpgradePeriod"=dword:8
"DeferUpdatePeriod"=dword:4

"ExcludeWUDriversInQualityUpdate"=dword:1
"FlightCommitted"=dword:0
; "FlightSettingsMaxPauseDays"=dword:000f4240
"FlightSettingsMaxPauseDays"=dword:99999999
"HideMCTLink"=dword:1
"InsiderProgramEnabled"=dword:0
"LastToastAction"=dword:0
"PauseDeferrals"=dword:1
"PauseFeatureUpdatesStartTime"="2015-05-05T05:05:05Z"
"PauseQualityUpdatesStartTime"="2015-05-05T05:05:05Z"
; Next 3 values below Delay/Defer/Pause/Postpone WU until 2077 (example), can be extended to any acceptable date:
"PauseUpdatesExpiryTime"="2077-07-07T07:07:07Z"
"PauseFeatureUpdatesEndTime"="2077-07-07T07:07:07Z"
"PauseQualityUpdatesEndTime"="2077-07-07T07:07:07Z"
"RestartNotificationsAllowed"=dword:1
"SetDisableUXWUAccess"=dword:1
"UxOption"=dword:0

Step 3:
*******
Get Microsoft SubInACL (SUBINACL.EXE) command line tool which displays/modifies/migrates NTFS Access Control List (ACL)
file system security options:
http://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=23510
File [MSI Installer]:
http://download.microsoft.com/download/1/7/d/17d82b72-bc6a-4dc8-bfaa-98b37b22b367/subinacl.msi
More info:
http://www.mdgx.com/xptoy.htm#SIA
http://www.mdgx.com/fmnt32/SUBINACL.HTM
Extract SubInACL (SUBINACL.EXE) to a folder/directory of your choice, preferably listed in your system PATH (example):
C:\WINDOWS\SYSTEM32
View your system path from a DOS console (command prompt) -> right-click CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE -> Run as Administrator ->
run this command -> press Enter:
SET PATH
Turn OFF ALL 4 Windows Update (WU) interconnected/interdependent/related services (+ stop BITS service temporarily) by
running BATch file below:
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text BATch (.bat) or CoMmanD (.cmd) script file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the BAT (.bat) or CMD (.cmd) extension.
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created BATch/CoMmanD file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Wait for completion.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
@ECHO OFF
IF NOT "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" GOTO END
:: Make sure SUBINACL.EXE resides in a folder listed in your system PATH -> see above.

SUBINACL.EXE /keyreg "HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services" /setowner=%UserName% /grant=%UserName%=f
SUBINACL.EXE /keyreg "HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services" /setowner=%UserName% /grant=%UserName%=f
SUBINACL.EXE /keyreg "HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services" /setowner=%UserName% /grant=%UserName%=f
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\BITS" BITS.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\BITS" BITS001.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\BITS" BITS002.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\DoSvc" Dosvc.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\DoSvc" Dosvc001.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\DoSvc" Dosvc002.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\UsoSvc" UsoSvc.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\UsoSvc" UsoSvc001.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\UsoSvc" UsoSvc002.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WaaSMedicSvc" WaaSMedicSvc.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WaaSMedicSvc" WaaSMedicSvc001.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WaaSMedicSvc" WaaSMedicSvc002.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\wuauserv" wuauserv.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\wuauserv" wuauserv001.reg /y
REG.EXE EXPORT "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\wuauserv" wuauserv002.reg /y
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\BITS\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\BITS\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\BITS\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\DoSvc\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\DoSvc\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\DoSvc\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\UsoSvc\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\UsoSvc\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\UsoSvc\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WaaSMedicSvc\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WaaSMedicSvc\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WaaSMedicSvc\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\wuauserv\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\wuauserv\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\wuauserv\Security" /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\BITS" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\BITS" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\BITS" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\DoSvc" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\DoSvc" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\DoSvc" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\UsoSvc" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\UsoSvc" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\UsoSvc" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WaaSMedicSvc" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WaaSMedicSvc" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WaaSMedicSvc" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\wuauserv" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\wuauserv" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f

REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WaaSMedicSvc" /v UserServiceFlags /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WaaSMedicSvc" /v UserServiceFlags /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WaaSMedicSvc" /v UserServiceFlags /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\wuauserv" /v UserServiceFlags /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\wuauserv" /v UserServiceFlags /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\wuauserv" /v UserServiceFlags /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\BITS" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 3 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\BITS" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 3 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\BITS" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 3 /f

REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\DoSvc" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\DoSvc" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\UsoSvc" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\UsoSvc" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\UsoSvc" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WaaSMedicSvc" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WaaSMedicSvc" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WaaSMedicSvc" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\wuauserv" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\wuauserv" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\wuauserv" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
ECHO Y|NET.EXE STOP BITS
SC.EXE CONFIG BITS START= demand
ECHO Y|NET.EXE STOP DoSvc
SC.EXE CONFIG DoSvc START= disabled
ECHO Y|NET.EXE STOP UsoSvc
SC.EXE CONFIG UsoSvc START= disabled
ECHO Y|NET.EXE STOP WaaSMedicSvc
SC.EXE CONFIG WaaSMedicSvc START= disabled

Step 4:
*******
Turn OFF ALL 4 (+ 1) Windows Update (WU) interconnected/interdependent/related services by running REG file below:
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
; Background Intelligent Transfer service (BITS):
; http://lifehacker.com/1786614642/
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\BITS\Security]
"Security"=hex:00
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\BITS\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\BITS]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:3
; Delivery Optimization service (DoSvc):
; http://www.techwibe.com/dosvc-bandwidth-eating-windows-10-permanent-solution-fix/
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\DoSvc\Security]
"Security"=hex:00
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\DoSvc\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\DoSvc]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:4
; Update Orchestrator service (UsoSvc):
; http://www.techwibe.com/what-does-usosvc-do-and-how-to-disable-usovsc/
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\UsoSvc\Security]
"Security"=hex:00
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\UsoSvc\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\UsoSvc]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:4
; Windows Update Medic service (WaaSMedicSvc):
; http://www.thewindowsclub.com/windows-update-blocker/
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WaaSMedicSvc\Security]
"Security"=hex:00
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WaaSMedicSvc\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WaaSMedicSvc]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:4

"LaunchProtected"=dword:0

"Start"=dword:4

"Security"=hex:00

"LaunchProtected"=dword:0

[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\UsoSvc]

[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WaaSMedicSvc\Security]

[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WaaSMedicSvc\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WaaSMedicSvc]

Step 5:
*******
Rename the %WinDir%\SoftwareDistribution [%WinDir% = usually C:\WINDOWS] folder to something else (example) by running
BATch file below:
http://tipsmake.com/how-to-change-the-download-folder-windows-update-in-windows-10
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text BATch (.bat) or CoMmanD (.cmd) script file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the BAT (.bat) or CMD (.cmd) extension.
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created BATch/CoMmanD file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Wait for completion.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
@ECHO OFF
IF NOT "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" GOTO END
TAKEOWN.EXE /f "%WinDir%\SoftwareDistribution" /r /d y
ICACLS.EXE "%WinDir%\SoftwareDistribution" /grant:r Everyone:F /t /c /q
REN "%WinDir%\SoftwareDistribution" SoftwareDistribution_OLD
:END
EXIT
------End cut & paste here------
OR delete the %WinDir%\SoftwareDistribution folder altogether (back it up first!) by running BATch file below:
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text BATch (.bat) or CoMmanD (.cmd) script file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the BAT (.bat) or CMD (.cmd) extension.
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created BATch/CoMmanD file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Wait for completion.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
@ECHO OFF
IF NOT "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" GOTO END
TAKEOWN.EXE /f "%WinDir%\SoftwareDistribution" /r /d y
ICACLS.EXE "%WinDir%\SoftwareDistribution" /grant:r Everyone:F /t /c /q
DEL /F /Q /S "%WinDir%\SoftwareDistribution\*.*"
RD /Q /S "%WinDir%\SoftwareDistribution"
:END
EXIT
------End cut & paste here------
Step 6:
*******
Rename all Windows Updates (WU) interconnected/interdependent/related scheduled tasks folders to any other names (example) by
running BATch file below:
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text BATch (.bat) or CoMmanD (.cmd) script file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the BAT (.bat) or CMD (.cmd) extension.
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created BATch/CoMmanD file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Wait for completion.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
@ECHO OFF
IF NOT "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" GOTO END
TAKEOWN.EXE /f "%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\UpdateOrchestrator" /r /d y
ICACLS.EXE "%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\UpdateOrchestrator" /grant:r Everyone:F /t /c /q
REN "%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\UpdateOrchestrator" UpdateOrchestrator_OLD
TAKEOWN.EXE /f "%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\WaaSMedic" /r /d y
ICACLS.EXE "%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\WaaSMedic" /grant:r Everyone:F /t /c /q
REN "%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\WaaSMedic" WaaSMedic_OLD
TAKEOWN.EXE /f "%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\WindowsUpdate" /r /d y
ICACLS.EXE "%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\WindowsUpdate" /grant:r Everyone:F /t /c /q
REN "%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Tasks\Microsoft\WINDOWS\WindowsUpdate" WindowsUpdate_OLD
:END
EXIT
------End cut & paste here------
Step 7 [last 1]:
****************
Last but not least, restart (reboot) Windows for all changes to take effect.

* SAFE INSTALL:
***************
* Install by hand/manually downloaded/local/offline individual/separate CAB/EXE/MSU Updates from Windows Updates Catalog (WUC)
in Windows 7/8/1.8/10:
http://woshub.com/manually-install-cab-msu-updates-windows/
This can be done even if Windows Update (WU) feature/service is blocked/disabled/turned OFF on your computer(s)/device(s), and
multiple such updates can be included in BATch (.bat)/CoMmanD (.cmd) files for automated/unattended install/upgrade purposes.
In case you add more than 1 such commands to the same batch file [.bat or .cmd], you should precede each command line with
"START /wait " (generic example):
START /wait WUSA.EXE "%UserProfile%\Downloads\No_Name_Update_1.msu" /quiet /norestart
START /wait WUSA.EXE "%UserProfile%\Downloads\No_Name_Update_2.msu" /quiet /norestart
START /wait WUSA.EXE "%UserProfile%\Downloads\No_Name_Update_3.msu" /quiet /norestart
Alternatively you can extract the main CAB (.cab) file (with identical/similar name as the MSU file) from the parent MSU (.msu)
installer using an unZIPping/unARChiving/unRARing tool [free(ware)]
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#ZIP
and install it from a DOS console (command prompt) -> right-click CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE -> Run as Administrator -> run this command
line (generic example: replace No_Name_Update below with the actual CAB file name):
DISM.EXE /Online /Add-Package /PackagePath:No_Name_Update.cab /Quiet /NoRestart
In case you run more than 1 such commands, or if you add more than 1 such commands to the same batch file [.bat or .cmd], you
should precede each command line with "START /wait " (generic example):
START /wait DISM.EXE /Online /Add-Package /PackagePath:No_Name_Update_1.cab /Quiet /NoRestart
START /wait DISM.EXE /Online /Add-Package /PackagePath:No_Name_Update_2.cab /Quiet /NoRestart
START /wait DISM.EXE /Online /Add-Package /PackagePath:No_Name_Update_3.cab /Quiet /NoRestart
NOTE:
See "Turn OFF/Postpone/Block/Uninstall Windows Updates (WU)" further above (this file), or go to:
http://www.mdgx.com/10.php
http://www.mdgx.com/WIN10.TXT
1. Search Windows Updates (WU) Catalog for the particular update(s) you wish to install (example):
http://www.catalog.update.microsoft.com/Search.aspx?q=cumulative%20x64%20windows%2010
Make sure the update(s) you select match the Windows NTx [7/8/8.1/2012/10/2016/2019/11/2022] operating system(s) [OS(es)] build(s),
edition(s) + bit strength [32-bit (x86) or 64-bit (x64)] you are using.
2. Download this file (example):
http://download.windowsupdate.com/c/msdownload/update/software/secu/2020/10/windows10.0-kb4579311-x64_9cc8221b0ed1bc799278d029c4edadf785920da9.msu
to your %UserProfile%\Downloads folder [default]:
%UserProfile%\Downloads\windows10.0-kb4579311-x64_9cc8221b0ed1bc799278d029c4edadf785920da9.msu
MSKB 4579311 Info:
http://support.microsoft.com/help/4579311/
MSKB 4579311 Downloads (from MS Catalog Update):
http://www.catalog.update.microsoft.com/search.aspx?q=KB4579311
MSKB 4579311 Bugs:
http://betanews.com/2020/10/17/windows-10-kb4579311-cumulative-update-problems/
3. Install the update you selected above from a DOS console (command prompt) -> right-click CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE ->
Run as Administrator -> run this command -> press Enter (example):
WUSA.EXE %UserProfile%\Downloads\windows10.0-kb4579311-x64_9cc8221b0ed1bc799278d029c4edadf785920da9.msu /quiet /norestart
4. Restart (reboot) Windows for all changes to take effect.

; operating systems are separate products."

; code used for Microsoft Edge web browser.
; https://opensource.org/faq/#commercial

1st Things 1st:
***************
BACKUP YOUR REGISTRY BEFORE MAKING ANY CHANGES! -> See "BACKUP/EXPORT + RESTORE/IMPORT REGISTRY/REGISTRY KEY(S)" in
WINDOWS7.TXT (included):
http://www.mdgx.com/7.php
http://www.mdgx.com/WINDOWS7.TXT
Example: I use winPenPack X-Chromium Portable 64-bit [free, open source]:
http://www.winpenpack.com/en/download.php?view.1082
also here:
http://sourceforge.net/projects/winpenpack/files/X-Chromium/releases/
On my gaming laptop the customized executables are located in these folders:
C:\PORT\CHROME\X-Chromium.exe
and respectively:
C:\PORT\CHROME\BIN\CHROME\CHROME.EXE
NOTE:
- Registry file below uses these values [example: I use winPenPack X-Chromium Portable = see above] to point to file names + their
respective locations. You need to replace them as needed to match your web browser executable(s) name(s) + location(s), depending
on the specific/custom program(s) you are using.
- All registry plain text strings [REG_SZ] listed here need to be replaced with the ones matching your existing/installed/registered
web browser(s). I use winPenPack X-Chromium Portable (example) -> see above:
Chrome
Chromium
Chromium web browser
X-Chromium
ChromeHTML
ChromiumHTML
winPenPack X-Chromium Launcher
winPenPack.X-ChromiumLauncher
winPenPack.X-ChromiumLauncher.Default
X-Chromium.File
XChromium.exe_.website
Chromium is a fast web browser for Windows.
C:\\PORT\\CHROME\\X-Chromium.exe
C:\\PORT\\CHROME\\BIN\\CHROME
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.

IMPORTANT:
In some cases you may need to change the default Microsoft web browser [IE or Edge] to match your favorite
existing/installed/registered web browser for (D)HTML/XML/PHP documents [.htm, .html, .dhtm, .dhtml, .xml, .php, .php4, .php5, etc]
by hand: Explorer -> right-click any of your local drives/partitions/volumes containing an .htm file (and then repeat same steps
for all other formats listed above) -> select Properties -> under Opens with: click "Change..." button -> under Other options click
"More apps |" -> in case your favorite web browser name is not listed scroll all the way to the bottom -> click "Look for another
app on this PC" -> scroll to your local drive/partition/volume (sub)folder where your favorite web browser executable (.exe) is
located -> double-click it -> click Open button -> click Apply button.
Change the default web browser to match your favorite existing/installed/registered web browser (examples):
http://www.androidauthority.com/how-to-change-the-default-browser-in-windows-10-987604/
http://support.google.com/chrome/answer/95417/
http://support.mozilla.org/kb/how-change-your-default-browser-windows-10/
http://www.computerworld.com/article/3229068/
http://www.cloudwards.net/how-to-disable-microsoft-edge/
http://support.microsoft.com/windows/change-your-default-browser-in-windows-10-020c58c6-7d77-797a-b74e-8f07946c5db6

1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Policies\DataCollection]
"Allow Telemetry"=dword:0
"AllowTelemetry"=dword:0
"DisableDeviceDelete"=-
"MaxTelemetryAllowed"=-
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Policies\Microsoft\Windows\DataCollection]
"Allow Telemetry"=dword:0
"AllowTelemetry"=dword:0
"DisableDeviceDelete"=-
"MaxTelemetryAllowed"=-

"DoNotTrack"=dword:1
[HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Policies\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main]
"DoNotTrack"=dword:1

Rename the %WinDir%\ServiceProfiles\LocalService\AppData\Local\Microsoft\NGC [%WinDir% = usually C:\WINDOWS] folder to
something else (example) by running BATch file below:
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text BATch (.bat) or CoMmanD (.cmd) script file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the BAT (.bat) or CMD (.cmd) extension.
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created BATch/CoMmanD file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Wait for completion.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
@ECHO OFF
IF NOT "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" GOTO END
TAKEOWN.EXE /f "%WinDir%\ServiceProfiles\LocalService\AppData\Local\Microsoft\NGC" /r /d y
ICACLS.EXE "%WinDir%\ServiceProfiles\LocalService\AppData\Local\Microsoft\NGC" /grant:r Everyone:F /t /c /q
REN "%WinDir%\ServiceProfiles\LocalService\AppData\Local\Microsoft\NGC" NGC_OLD
:END
EXIT
------End cut & paste here------

Services that refuse to be disabled or to have their status changed from within SERVICES.MSC can be disabled/(re)enabled using the
Registry Editor (RegEdit): right-click RegEdit (%WinDir%\REGEDIT.EXE) [%WinDir% = usually C:\WINDOWS] or its shortcut/link ->
Run as Administrator -> go to this registry key
HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services
-> click left hand pane desired service name registry key [example: Dnscache]
HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\Dnscache
-> double-click right hand pane "Start" DWORD [REG_DWORD] registry value -> change its numeric value to 4 [which means Disabled] ->
press OK -> exit RegEdit.
IMPORTANT:
**********
- Your custom/specific needs/choices/preferences/settings and devices/hardware/software/services for specific pairs/batches/groups
of interconnected/interdependent/related services may be different depeding on what you do with your computer(s)/portable(s)/device(s),
and/or what (combination of) devices/hardware/software/services you are using.
- Make sure to review carefully each service documentation, and most importantly each service "Dependencies" tab as shown in
SERVICES.MSC *before* disabling them (example):
http://www.thewindowsclub.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/05/Windows-10-Service-Dependencies.png
NOTE:
*****
Windows 10 introduced a new "breed" of Windows services: Per-User services, marked at the end of the name string with an
underscore (_) or a space ( ) followed by a 4-12 digit numeric string [Locally Unique IDentifier (LUID)], which is unique for each user
and/or each user session/login/up time, depending on which Windows 10 build/edition/update you are using.
http://docs.microsoft.com/windows/application-management/per-user-services-in-windows/
http://helgeklein.com/blog/per-user-services-in-windows-info-and-configuration/
1st Things 1st:
***************
BACKUP YOUR REGISTRY BEFORE MAKING ANY CHANGES! -> See "BACKUP/EXPORT + RESTORE/IMPORT REGISTRY/REGISTRY KEY(S)" in
WINDOWS7.TXT (included):
http://www.mdgx.com/7.php
http://www.mdgx.com/WINDOWS7.TXT
Per-User services can be disabled and/or prevented from being (re)created by changing their default "LaunchProtected", "Security" and/or
"UserServiceFlags" registry DWORD [REG_DWORD] 32-bit or Binary [REG_BINARY] numeric values to null [dword:0 or hex:00/hex(0):] (examples):
http://docs.microsoft.com/answers/questions/401557/
See the "Registry Structure" section under "Comprehensive Windows Registry Guide" chapter in REGISTRY.TXT (included), also online:
http://www.mdgx.com/reg.htm#RTS
CAUTION:
Disabling/changing some of these registry keys/values may impair/limit normal/proper Windows functionality/operation, cause errors, or
even lock you out of your Windows Operating System (OS)!
Make sure you already have a current full Windows backup copy and backups of all main registry keys saved in binary format *before* making
any changes = see "BACKUP/EXPORT + RESTORE/IMPORT REGISTRY/REGISTRY KEY(S)" in WINDOWS7.TXT (included):
http://www.mdgx.com/7.php
http://www.mdgx.com/WINDOWS7.TXT
Only after that...
******************
Plan A
~~~~~~
Disable Per-User service [WpnUserService] from a DOS console (command prompt) -> right-click CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE -> Run as Administrator
-> run these commands -> press Enter after each line (example):
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WpnUserService\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WpnUserService\Security" /f
REG.EXE DELETE "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WpnUserService\Security" /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WpnUserService\Security" /v Security /t REG_BINARY /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WpnUserService\Security" /v Security /t REG_BINARY /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WpnUserService\Security" /v Security /t REG_BINARY /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WpnUserService" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WpnUserService" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WpnUserService" /v LaunchProtected /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WpnUserService" /v UserServiceFlags /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WpnUserService" /v UserServiceFlags /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WpnUserService" /v UserServiceFlags /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WpnUserService" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WpnUserService" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKLM\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WpnUserService" /v Start /t REG_DWORD /d 4 /f
OR if method above does not work (using same example):
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WpnUserService\Security]
"Security"=hex:00
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WpnUserService\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\WpnUserService]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WpnUserService\Security]
"Security"=hex:00
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WpnUserService\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\WpnUserService]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WpnUserService\Security]
"Security"=hex:00
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WpnUserService\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\WpnUserService]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:4
;
------End cut & paste here------
Plan B
~~~~~~
In case both methods above do not work due to Windows 10 registry protection, you may need to do this by hand by using the Registry
Editor (%WinDir%\RegEdit.exe) [%WinDir% = usually C:\WINDOWS] (using same example): right-click RegEdit or its shortcut/link ->
Run as Administrator -> go to this registry key:
HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services
and then to this registry key:
HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services
and then to this registry key (if present):
HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services
-> click left hand pane desired service name registry key [example: WpnUserService] (if present) -> double-click right hand pane
"Start" DWORD [REG_DWORD] registry value -> change its numeric value to 4 [which means Disabled]-> press OK -> exit RegEdit.
Repeat same steps for the other registry values above and set their DWORD [REG_DWORD] or Binary [REG_BINARY] numeric values to null
[dword:0 or hex:00 or hex(0):] (see above):
LaunchProtected [REG_DWORD] = dword:0
Security [REG_BINARY] = hex:00 [hex(0):]
UserServiceFlags [REG_DWORD] = dword:0
Plan C
~~~~~~
In case "Plan B" above does not work due to Windows 10 registry protection, you can do this by hand by running the Registry Editor
(%WinDir%\RegEdit.exe) [%WinDir% = usually C:\WINDOWS] as TrustedInstaller (highest available user level) using AdvancedRun.exe
(example):
AdvancedRun.exe /EXEFilename "%windir%\REGEDIT.EXE" /RunAs 8 /Run
AdvancedRun (AdvancedRun.exe) 32-bit + 64-bit GUI interface + DOS console command line tool for Windows Vista/7/8/8.1/10
32-bit + 64-bit runs any app/batch/command/executable/function/process/program/script/service/task/tool as
Administrator/SYSTEM/TrustedInstaller/any user with elevated/highest/protected privileges/rights, compatibility,
environment, ownership, permissions, priority, properties, useful for task automation in BATch (.BAT), CoMmanD (.CMD) +
Visual Basic Script (.VBS) files, highly customizable:
http://www.nirsoft.net/utils/advanced_run.html
AdvancedRun 64-bit:
http://www.nirsoft.net/utils/advancedrun-x64.zip
AdvancedRun 32-bit:
http://www.nirsoft.net/utils/advancedrun.zip
Run Programs as SYSTEM:
http://www.winhelponline.com/blog/run-program-as-system-localsystem-account-windows/
Run Programs as TrustedInstaller:
http://www.winhelponline.com/blog/run-program-as-trustedinstaller-locked-registry-keys-files/
As soon as the RegEdit window is open, repeat all steps above from "Plan B".
Example: Windows Defender Antivirus Service [WinDefend] can be disabled only by using RegEdit as TrustedInstaller, or if you're
running a Windows 10 edition other than Home, it may still be available by running Group Policy Editor (GPEdit.msc).
http://tipsmake.com/instructions-to-turn-off-windows-defender-completely-on-windows-10

Final Step
~~~~~~~~~~
No matter which "Plan" you have used, you should restart (reboot) Windows for all changes to take effect.

services, devices, drivers, functions, apps/programs, residents, and/or tasks]:
AVCTP service [BthAvctpSvc]
Bluetooth Audio Gateway Service [BTAGService]

Windows Settings (WS) + Control Panel (CP) Shortcuts



* Create Windows 10 Windows Settings (WS) a.k.a. Immersive Control Panel (ICP) a.k.a. native Control Panel + Metro/Tile/Store/UWP
apps/programs/games/tools command(s) shortcut(s) (.lnk, .url): Desktop (empty spot) -> right-click -> New -> Shortcut ->
cut & paste respective "ms-settings:xxxx" text string listed below [not all are available, some may differ depending on installed
Windows OS edition/update(s) and/or installed apps/features/programs/games/tools and/or configuration/settings]:
http://docs.microsoft.com/windows/uwp/launch-resume/launch-settings-app/
See also my Windows 10 Settings Uniform Resource Identifier (URI) commands links/shortcuts listed in WIN10SET.HTM (included):
http://www.mdgx.com/WIN10SET.HTM
Similar resources:
http://www.majorgeeks.com/content/page/how_to_create_a_shortcut_to_any_windows_settings.html
http://tenop.com/windows-10-settings-links-launch-list-guide/

To access any of these Uniform Resource Identifier (URI) links/shortcuts: make sure you're logged in with
Administrator/Sysadmin/SYSTEM privileges -> Run... [hold WinKey + press R] -> type this command:
ms-settings:
-> press Enter.
OR this command:
EXPLORER.EXE ms-settings:
-> press Enter.

1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.

Uninstall/Remove Quick Assist app:
http://walkersam.blogspot.com/2017/10/how-to-uninstall-quick-assist-within.html
http://github.com/adolfintel/Windows10-Privacy/issues/37/
Right-click PowerShell shortcut or C:\WINDOWS\System32\WindowsPowerShell\v1.0\PowerShell.exe [default location] -> Run as Administrator
-> run this command -> press Enter:
PowerShell.exe -ExecutionPolicy Unrestricted
Then from within the PowerShell console run this command -> press Enter:
Remove-WindowsCapability -online -name App.Support.QuickAssist~~~~0.0.1.0
OR this command -> press Enter:
Get-WindowsPackage -Online | Where PackageName -like *QuickAssist* | Remove-WindowsPackage -Online -NoRestart
Uninstall/Remove Microsoft Hello Face + Hello for Business apps:
http://dirteam.com/sander/2020/07/02/howto-delete-your-windows-hello-for-business-registration/
http://github.com/adolfintel/Windows10-Privacy/issues/37/
Right-click CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE -> Run as Administrator -> run this command -> press Enter:
certutil.exe -DeleteHelloContainer
Right-click PowerShell shortcut or C:\WINDOWS\System32\WindowsPowerShell\v1.0\PowerShell.exe [default location] -> Run as Administrator
-> run this command -> press Enter:
PowerShell.exe -ExecutionPolicy Unrestricted
Then from within the PowerShell console run this command -> press Enter:
Get-WindowsPackage -Online | Where PackageName -like *Hello-Face* | Remove-WindowsPackage -Online -NoRestart
Uninstall/Remove Contact Support + Feedback (Hub) apps:

http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#ZIP
to open "Uninstall_Contact_Support.zip" archive and extract "Uninstall Contact Support.cmd" + "install_wim_tweak.exe" into the same
dedicated/empty directory/folder -> right-click "Uninstall Contact Support.cmd" -> Run as Administrator -> reboot.

* Turn ON Prefetch, SuperFetch + SysMain services to speed up loading of frequently used executables (.exe) in Windows 7/8/8.1/10:
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/99821-enable-disable-superfetch-windows.html
http://www.technipages.com/windows-enable-disable-superfetch/

1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\FileInfo\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\FileInfo]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:2
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\RpcSs\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\RpcSs]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:2
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\SysMain\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\SysMain]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:2
"SvcMemHardLimitInMB"=dword:002dc6c0
"SvcMemMidLimitInMB"=dword:0000012c
"SvcMemSoftLimitInMB"=dword:0000001e
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Session Manager\Memory Management\PrefetchParameters]
"EnableSuperfetch"=dword:3
"EnablePrefetcher"=dword:3
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\FileInfo\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\FileInfo]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:2
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\RpcSs\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\RpcSs]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:2
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\SysMain\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\SysMain]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:2
"SvcMemHardLimitInMB"=dword:002dc6c0
"SvcMemMidLimitInMB"=dword:0000012c
"SvcMemSoftLimitInMB"=dword:0000001e
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Control\Session Manager\Memory Management\PrefetchParameters]
"EnableSuperfetch"=dword:3
"EnablePrefetcher"=dword:3
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\FileInfo\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\FileInfo]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"UserServiceFlags"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:2

* Turn OFF Network Location Awareness (NLA) service (NlaSvc) Active Probing + Network Connectivity Status Indicator (NCSI) Taskbar
icon in Windows 8/8.1/10:
http://support.microsoft.com/help/4494446/
http://newsignature.com/articles/network-location-awareness-service-can-ruin-day-fix/
http://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/winsock/network-location-awareness-service-provider-nla--2/
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\NlaSvc\Parameters\Internet]
"EnableActiveProbing"=dword:0
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\NlaSvc\Parameters\Internet]
"EnableActiveProbing"=dword:0
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\NlaSvc\Parameters\Internet]
"EnableActiveProbing"=dword:0
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Policies\Microsoft\Windows\NetworkConnectivityStatusIndicator]
"DisablePassivePolling"=dword:1
"NoActiveProbe"=dword:1
;
------End cut & paste here------
BUG:
****
Your active/current/installed internet/network/LAN/WAN/Wi-Fi/wireless connection might report this false error
(NCSI Taskbar icon):
"No Internet"
even if it works properly.
http://superuser.com/questions/1400187/
FIX:
****
In such cases you can (re)enable these 2 registry values:
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Policies\Microsoft\Windows\NetworkConnectivityStatusIndicator]
"DisablePassivePolling"=dword:0
"NoActiveProbe"=dword:0
;
------End cut & paste here------
Restart (reboot) Windows for these changes to take effect.

Install NEWest available version of Microsoft .Net Framework Redistributable (NFR):

1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.

"LongPathsEnabled"=dword:1

"LongPathsEnabled"=dword:1

"LongPathsEnabled"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Control\FileSystem]
"LongPathsEnabled"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Policies]
"LongPathsEnabled"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Control\FileSystem]
"LongPathsEnabled"=dword:1
[HKEY_CURRENT_USER\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Group Policy Objects\{48981759-12F2-42A6-A048-028B3973495F}Machine\System\CurrentControlSet\Policies]
"LongPathsEnabled"=dword:1
[HKEY_USERS\.DEFAULT\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Group Policy Objects\{48981759-12F2-42A6-A048-028B3973495F}Machine\System\CurrentControlSet\Policies]
"LongPathsEnabled"=dword:1
;
------End cut & paste here------

LIMITATION:
Desktop/Explorer/icon/item/link/shortcut/context/shell/right-click submenus (see "||==== Windows Settings (WS) = NATIVE ====>"
item = see example JPEG screen above) allow a maximum of 16 items each in all Windows NTx editions/releases.
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.

* Switch between Windows System, Shell + Windows Apps Dark [Side ;-/] + Light [Force ;-/] Modes:
http://www.windowscentral.com/how-switch-between-light-and-dark-colors-schedule-automatically-windows-10/
http://www.laptopmag.com/articles/windows-10-dark-theme/
http://www.laptopmag.com/articles/enable-light-mode-windows-10/
http://www.digitalcitizen.life/how-enable-disable-dark-mode-windows-10/
http://www.pcmag.com/how-to/how-to-enable-dark-mode-in-windows-10/
Start button/logo/orb -> Settings -> Personalization [Background, Lock Screen, Colors] -> left hand Colors menu
EXPLORER.EXE ms-settings:personalization-colors
-> Choose your color drop down menu -> Dark (example).
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text BATch (.bat) or CoMmanD (.cmd) script file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the BAT (.bat) or CMD (.cmd) extension.
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created BATch/CoMmanD file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Wait for completion.
Turn ON The Dark "Side" Mode batch file:
"If you only knew the power of the Dark Side." ;-/
http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=esEcwAWi6dk
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
@ECHO OFF
IF NOT "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" GOTO END
:: Turn ON The Dark "Side" Mode:
REG.EXE ADD "HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Themes\Personalize" /v SystemUsesLightTheme /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Themes\Personalize" /v AppsUseLightTheme /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKU\.DEFAULT\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Themes\Personalize" /v SystemUsesLightTheme /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKU\.DEFAULT\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Themes\Personalize" /v AppsUseLightTheme /t REG_DWORD /d 0 /f
:END
EXIT
------End cut & paste here------
Turn ON The Light "Force" Mode batch file:
"The Force will be with you. Always." ;-/
http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ycCAHYvAUl4
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
@ECHO OFF
IF NOT "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" GOTO END
:: Turn ON The Light "Force" Mode:
REG.EXE ADD "HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Themes\Personalize" /v SystemUsesLightTheme /t REG_DWORD /d 1 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Themes\Personalize" /v AppsUseLightTheme /t REG_DWORD /d 1 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKU\.DEFAULT\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Themes\Personalize" /v SystemUsesLightTheme /t REG_DWORD /d 1 /f
REG.EXE ADD "HKU\.DEFAULT\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Themes\Personalize" /v AppsUseLightTheme /t REG_DWORD /d 1 /f
:END
EXIT
------End cut & paste here------

* Turn OFF unnecessary, obsolete + unsafe TCP/IP NetBIOS (Network Basic Input/Output System) Helper service [lmhosts] + NetBIOS
over TCP/IP (NetBT, NBT) protocol for internet connections IF not using NetBT/NBT networks +/- sharing data/files/printers over
internet/networks using OLDer/obsolete NetBT/NBT protocol:
http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/NetBIOS_over_TCP/IP
http://windowsreport.com/how-to-disable-netbios/
http://support.microsoft.com/help/313314/
http://10dsecurity.com/saying-goodbye-netbios/
http://technet.microsoft.com/library/cc940063.aspx
http://support.hidemyass.com/hc/articles/202720396/
http://www.techrepublic.com/blog/it-security/the-problem-with-netbios/
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT

Run Control Panel (CP) Network + Internet Center -> Run... [hold WinKey + press R] -> type:
CONTROL.EXE /name Microsoft.NetworkAndSharingCenter
-> press Enter -> (double-)click your active/running broadband/cable/Ethernet/local/satellite/internet/network/LAN/WAN/NIC/Wi-Fi/wireless/etc
connection icon -> Properties button -> Networking tab -> This connection is using the following items: -> Internet Protocol Version 4
(TCP/IPv4) -> General tab -> Advanced... button -> WINS tab -> check Enable LMHOSTS lookup box -> NetBIOS setting -> check Disable NetBIOS
over TCP/IP box -> Apply/OK.

Pin to Taskbar Command Prompt Utility (syspin.exe) 64-bit for Windows 7/8/8.1/10 64-bit:
http://www.technosys.net/products/utils/pintotaskbar
File:
http://www.technosys.net/download.aspx?file=syspin.exe
syspin.exe command line parameters:
http://www.technosys.net/images/products/syspin1.jpg
-------snip-------
Usage:
syspin ["file"] ### or syspin ["file"] "commandstring"
5386 : Pin to taskbar
5387 : Unpin from taskbar
51261 : Pin to start
51394 : Unpin to start
Samples:
syspin "%PROGRAMFILES%\Internet Explorer\iexplore.exe" 5386
syspin "C:\Windows\notepad.exe" "Pin to taskbar"
syspin "%WINDIR%\System32\calc.exe" "Pin to start"
syspin "%WINDIR%\System32\calc.exe" "Unpin from taskbar"
syspin "C:\Windows\System32\calc.exe" 51201
Note: You cannot pin any metro app or batch file
-------snip-------
Add "Pin File/Item to Taskbar = SysPin (syspin.exe) 64-bit" item to the right-click shell context menu for all file types [*]
(I have used C:\TOOLS_10 folder in this example):
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Classes\*\shell\Pin_syspin64]
@="Pin File/Item to Taskbar = SysPin (syspin.exe) 64-bit"
"SuppressionPolicy"=dword:0
"Icon"="\"C:\\TOOLS_10\\syspin.exe\",0"
"NoWorkingDirectory"=""
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Classes\*\shell\Pin_syspin64\command]
@="\"C:\\TOOLS_10\\syspin.exe\" \"%1\" 5386"
"IsolatedCommand"=-
;
------End cut & paste here------

Right-click PowerShell shortcut or C:\WINDOWS\System32\WindowsPowerShell\v1.0\PowerShell.exe [default location] -> Run as Administrator
-> run this command -> press Enter:
PowerShell.exe -ExecutionPolicy Unrestricted
After PowerShell console comes up -> run this command -> press Enter:
Get-AppXPackage -AllUsers | Foreach {Add-AppXPackage -DisableDevelopmentMode -Register "$($_.InstallLocation)\AppXManifest.xml"}
-> exit PowerShell.
Restart (reboot) Windows for these changes to take effect.

* Turn OFF Narrator, start before/after sign-in, quick start, keyboard shortcuts + online services in Windows 7/8/8.1/10:
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/88188-turn-off-narrator-windows-10-a.html
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/113745-turn-off-start-narrator-after-sign-windows-10-a.html
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/120822-turn-off-narrator-caps-lock-warnings-while-typing-windows-10-a.html
http://www.winaero.com/disable-narrator-home-in-windows-10/
http://www.winaero.com/download-start-narrator-before-sign-in/
http://www.winaero.com/disable-narrator-keyboard-shortcut-windows-10/
http://www.winaero.com/disable-narrator-quickstart-guide-windows-10/
http://www.winaero.com/start-narrator-before-sign-windows-10/
http://www.howtoedge.com/disable-online-services-for-narrator-in-windows-10/
http://www.pcerror-fix.com/complete-steps-to-disable-and-enable-narrator-in-windows-10/
Access Narrator settings: Run... [hold WinKey + press R] -> type this command:
ms-settings:easeofaccess-narrator
-> press Enter -> turn OFF/ON or tweak the ones you want.
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Narrator\NoRoam]
"CapsLockAlert"=dword:2
"OnlineServicesEnabled"=dword:0
"WinEnterLaunchEnabled"=dword:0
[HKEY_USERS\.DEFAULT\Software\Microsoft\Narrator\NoRoam]
"CapsLockAlert"=dword:2
"WinEnterLaunchEnabled"=dword:0
"OnlineServicesEnabled"=dword:0
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows NT\CurrentVersion\Accessibility]
"Configuration"=""
[HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Windows NT\CurrentVersion\Accessibility]
"Configuration"=""
[HKEY_USERS\.DEFAULT\Software\Microsoft\Windows NT\CurrentVersion\Accessibility]
"Configuration"=""
[HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Narrator\NarratorHome]
"AutoStart"=dword:0
[HKEY_USERS\.DEFAULT\Software\Microsoft\Narrator\NarratorHome]
"AutoStart"=dword:0
[HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Narrator\QuickStart]
"SkipQuickStart"=dword:1
[HKEY_USERS\.DEFAULT\Software\Microsoft\Narrator\QuickStart]
"SkipQuickStart"=dword:1
;
------End cut & paste here------

* Turn OFF + Uninstall Miracast Connect Receiver (Connect app) + Project to this PC in Windows 10:
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/49088-change-when-ask-project-pc-windows-10-a.html
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/49466-enable-disable-projecting-pc-windows-10-a.html
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/157692-install-uninstall-connect-wireless-display-feature-windows-10-a.html
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\MiracastReceiver]
"ConsentToast"=dword:0
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Policies\Microsoft\Windows\Connect]
"AllowProjectionToPC"=dword:0
;
------End cut & paste here------
Uninstall Miracast Connect Receiver (Connect app) from a DOS console (command prompt) -> right-click CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE ->
Run as Administrator -> run this command -> press Enter:
DISM.EXE /Online /Remove-Capability /CapabilityName:App.WirelessDisplay.Connect~~~~0.0.1.0

http://superuser.com/questions/1506090/
http://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/shell/knownfolderid/

* Save/Export + Restore/Import custom Power plan/scheme settings in Windows 10:
http://www.winaero.com/save-power-plan-settings-text-file-windows-10/
http://www.winaero.com/export-import-power-plan-windows-10/
http://docs.microsoft.com/windows-hardware/design/device-experiences/powercfg-command-line-options/
http://technet.microsoft.com/library/cc748940.aspx
http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Powercfg
http://www.ss64.com/nt/powercfg.html
http://web.archive.org/web/20080212041212/http://xpregistry.uw.hu/xpr0035.html
Perform all these operations from a DOS console (command prompt) -> right-click CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE -> Run as Administrator
-> run these commands -> press Enter after each line (examples):
Save/export active Power scheme custom settings details to text file (example):
POWERCFG.EXE /QH>C:\POWER_10\POWER_10.TXT
Save/export active Power Scheme Global Unique ID (GUID) number to text file (example):
POWERCFG.EXE /L>C:\POWER_10\POWER_10_GUID.TXT
Export/save active Power scheme custom settings to binary file [replace GUID_# below with your actual GUID_# number from
POWER_10_GUID.TXT text file above] (example):
POWERCFG.EXE /EXPORT "C:\POWER_10\POWER_10.POW" GUID_#
Import/restore Power scheme custom settings from POWER_10.POW binary file above:
POWERCFG.EXE /IMPORT "C:\POWER_10\POWER_10.POW"

PCs/laptops/portables/tablets/devices with Windows 10 preinstalled can be reset to factory defaults: login screen -> Power button ->
hold Shift + click Restart button -> Troubleshoot button -> Reset this PC button -> Keep my files button -> this reinstalls Windows 10,
resets all system settings to their defaults, and keeps all your files/folders/some user setttings, desktop icons, and some of your
custom settings +/- changes -> Reboot normal.
In case this doesn't work, or if you have been locked out of your computer -> Power button -> F9 or F12 (depending on your computer
brand + model) -> BIOS Setup -> Boot tab/screen -> Windows Boot Manager button/item -> Enter -> Recovery -> See advanced repair
options button -> Troubleshoot button -> Reset this PC button -> Keep my files button -> reinstall Windows 10 (see above) -> Reboot
normal.
Afterwards you may need to customize (some of) your system/user settings, and reinstall your 3rd party/custom
programs/apps/drivers/items and eventually customize them from scratch.

Backup + Restore TileDataLayer database (.edb) using a BATch file:
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text BATch (.bat) or CoMmanD (.cmd) script file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the BAT (.bat) or CMD (.cmd) extension.
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created BATch/CoMmanD file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Wait for completion.
I. Backup TileDataLayer database (.edb):
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
@ECHO OFF
IF NOT "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" GOTO END
TASKKILL.EXE /IM EXPLORER.EXE /F
C:
CD "C:\Users\%UserName%\AppData\Local\TileDataLayer\Database"
SC.EXE STOP tiledatamodelsvc
MD "%UserProfile%\Desktop\StartMenuBAK"
COPY /Y *.* "%UserProfile%\Desktop\StartMenuBAK"
DEL /F /Q *.*
SC.EXE START tiledatamodelsvc
EXPLORER.EXE
:END
EXIT
------End cut & paste here------
II. Restore TileDataLayer database (.edb):
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
@ECHO OFF
IF NOT "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" GOTO END
TASKKILL.EXE /IM EXPLORER.EXE /F
C:
CD "C:\Users\%UserName%\AppData\Local\TileDataLayer\Database"
SC.EXE STOP tiledatamodelsvc
COPY /Y "%UserProfile%\Desktop\StartMenuBAK\*.*"
SC.EXE START tiledatamodelsvc
EXPLORER.EXE
:END
EXIT
------End cut & paste here------
Backup TileDataLayer database (.edb) + related files + folders:
http://www.exefiles.com/en/edb/vedatamodel-edb/
http://superuser.com/questions/1194556/
List of files + folders:
%UserProfile%\AppData\Local\TileDataLayer\Database\vedatamodel.edb
%WinDir%\ImmersiveControlPanel\Application.manifest
%UserProfile%\AppData\Local\Microsoft\Windows\CloudStore
%UserProfile%\AppData\Local\Microsoft\Windows\Caches
%UserProfile%\AppData\Local\Microsoft\Windows\Explorer
Right-click PowerShell shortcut or C:\WINDOWS\System32\WindowsPowerShell\v1.0\PowerShell.exe [default location] -> Run as
Administrator -> run these commands -> press Enter after each line:

Export-StartLayout -Path C:\StartLayoutBAK\start.xml
Import-StartLayout -LayoutPath .\start.xml -MountPath C:\StartLayoutBAK

[32-bit (x86) +/- 64-bit (x64)] you are using:

Copy tdlrecover.exe to %WinDir%\SYSTEM32 (only if not present; do NOT overwrite it if present!) from a DOS console (command
prompt) -> right-click CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE -> Run as Administrator -> run this command -> press Enter (using default folder
names):
COPY "%UserProfile%\Downloads\tdlrecover.exe" %WinDir%\SYSTEM32
Run... [hold WinKey + press R] -> type:
%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\tdlrecover.exe -reregister -resetlayout -resetcache
-> press Enter.

* FIX: Windows 7/8/8.1/10 NVidia Control Panel optimal settings on laptops/portables with dual GPUs (most likely DCH in Windows 10)
[example: Intel (primary) + NVidia (secondary)] to avoid annoying apps/programs/games/savers/etc (especially web browsers,
multimedia 3D/audio/video players/editors/managers, image viewers/editors/managers, games, screen savers) that sometimes (by default)
select the wrong, built-in/integrated, least powerful (Power Saving) graphics processor for software hungry for hardware resources,
and sometimes reset/switch (between) different GPUs/video modes and reset the active display/monitor unexpectedly, blanking out the
screen for a few seconds, especially in the middle of performing critical/essential/vital/important work:
http://i.imgur.com/SZRQoe2.jpg
http://www.howtogeek.com/351522/
http://www.dell.com/support/kbdoc/en-us/000178995/
http://support.lenovo.com/us/en/solutions/ht071102/
NVidia Declarative Componentized Hardware (DCH) [say that 10 times fast! ;-/] Graphic Drivers for Windows 10:
http://nvidia.custhelp.com/app/answers/detail/a_id/4777/
Right-click an empty spot on your Desktop -> select NVidia Control Panel (most likely DCH in Windows 10) or (Windows 10 users only):
run Windows 10 Settings (WS) -> Display ->
http://www.mdgx.com/WIN10SET.HTM
Run... [hold WinKey + press R] -> type this command:
ms-settings:display
-> press Enter.
All Windows 7/8/8.1/10 users -> go to:
- 3D Settings -> Configure Surround, PhysX -> PhysX settings -> Processor: -> GeForce/Quadro/Titan GTX/RTX xxxx/Xyyyy -> Apply/OK.
- 3D Settings -> Global Settings -> Preferred graphics processor: -> High-performance NVidia processor -> Apply/OK.
- 3D Settings -> Program settings -> 1. Select a program to customize: -> browse to select a program/app/game/tool -> 2. Select the
preferred graphics processor for this program: -> High-performance NVidia processor (if available or possible) -> Apply/OK.
- Display -> Adjust Desktop Color Settings -> Content type reported to the display: -> Auto-select (recommended) -> Apply/OK.
- Display -> Adjust Desktop Size and Position -> Size -> Select the desktop resize mode reported to the display: -> Auto-select
(recommended) -> Apply/OK.
- Display -> Change Resolution -> 3. Apply the following settings. -> check Use NVidia color settings box -> Desktop color depth: ->
Highest (32-bit) -> Output color depth: -> 10 bpc (or highest avaiable) -> Output color format: -> RGB -> Output dynamic range: ->
Full (0-255) -> Apply/OK.
Run NVidia Control Panel (most likely DCH in Windows 10) app/executable/shortcut -> Multiple Displays -> press Detect button -> your
monitor name + model/type should appear -> Advanced Display Settings -> Choose display -> Select a display to view or change the
settings for it. -> Display adapter properties for Display # [1, 2, etc] -> Monitor tab -> Monitor Settings -> Screen refresh rate:
-> select highest refresh rate available for your monitor from the list -> Apply/OK.
