* FIX: Force apps/programs/games/tools to use high performance NVidia GPU (Graphics Processing Unit) processor and play/render
video/movie/CD/DVD/BD/etc multimedia file types properly on laptops/portables with 2 GPUs [Intel + NVidia] in Windows 10.
Example using Media Player Classic Home Cinema (MPC-HC) multimedia player [MPC-HC.exe 32-bit or MPC-HC64.exe 64-bit] installed by
K-Lite Codec Pack (KLCP) Mega 32-bit or 64-bit:
http://www.codecguide.com/faq_mpc.htm#item44
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/103965-set-preferred-gpu-apps-windows-10-a.html
K-Lite Codec Pack (KLCP) Mega [free(ware)]:
http://www.codecguide.com/download_k-lite_codec_pack_mega.htm
1. MPC-HC(64) -> pause file playback (if any) -> right-click -> Options (O) -> Playback -> Output -> DirectShow Video [H/W] ->
Enhanced Video Renderer (EVR) -> Apply/OK.
http://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/directshow/video-mixing-renderer-filter-9/
2. MPC-HC(64) -> pause file playback (if any) -> click red LAV Video Decoder Taskbar icon -> Hardware Acceleration [H/W] ->
Hardware Decoder to use: -> DXVA2 (DirectX Video Acceleration 2) (copy-back) -> Hardware Device to use: -> NVidia GeForce (GTX)
xxxx (example) [*only* if your laptop/portable is using an external connected display/monitor/screen/TV as *primary* display!] ->
check *all* Resolutions + Codecs boxes *except* DVD, MPEG-2 + VC-1 -> Apply/OK.
http://anime.my/tutorials/watching-h264-videos-using-compute-unified-device-architecture-cuda/
madVR Tutorial:
http://anime.my/tutorials/madvr/
Use NVIDIA Profile Inspector (NPI) -> modify Media Player Classic Home Cinema [MPC-HC(64).exe] profile:
http://www.guru3d.com/files-details/nvidia-profile-inspector-download.html
Enable application for Optimus = SHIM_RENDERING_MODE_ENABLE (0x00000001)
1. Copy under a different name or rename your default multimedia video/movie player associated with video/movie/CD/DVD/BD/etc file types,
in this case Media Player Classic Home Cinema [MPC-HC] executable [MPC-HC.exe 32-bit or MPC-HC64.exe 64-bit] installed by
K-Lite Codec Pack (KLCP) Mega 32-bit or 64-bit,
http://www.codecguide.com/download_k-lite_codec_pack_mega.htm
to something else (example using default KLCP install folders) from a DOS console (command prompt) -> right-click CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE ->
Run as Administrator -> run 1 of the commands below depending on your Windows NTx edition: 64-bit (x64) or 32-bit (x86) -> press Enter
(example):
- Windows NTx 64-bit (x64):
COPY /Y "C:\Program Files (x86)\K-Lite Codec Pack\MPC-HC64\mpc-hc64.exe" "C:\Program Files (x86)\K-Lite Codec Pack\MPC-HC64\MPC-HC64_NV.exe"
- Windows NTx 32-bit (x86):
COPY /Y "C:\Program Files\K-Lite Codec Pack\MPC-HC\mpc-hc.exe" "C:\Program Files\K-Lite Codec Pack\MPC-HC\MPC-HC_NV.exe"
2. Right-click an empty spot on your Desktop -> click NVidia Control Panel -> Manage 3D Settings -> Program Settings tab -> Add button ->
Browse... button -> depending on your Windows NTx edition: 64-bit (x64) or 32-bit (x86) go to:
- Windows NTx 64-bit (x64):
C:\Program Files (x86)\K-Lite Codec Pack\MPC-HC64\MPC-HC64_NV.exe
- Windows NTx 32-bit (x86):
C:\Program Files\K-Lite Codec Pack\MPC-HC\MPC-HC_NV.exe
-> double-click it -> under Select the preferred graphics processor for this program: -> select High-performance NVidia processor ->
Apply/OK button.
3. Make this new MPC-HC(64) executable your new default multimedia player: associate it with your video/movie/CD/DVD/BD/etc file types from
within MPC-HC(64) interface: pause file playback (if any) -> press O -> Options -> Player -> Formats -> File extensions -> check the boxes
for your desired audio/video format(s) -> Apply/OK.

* Tweak Timeout Detection and Recovery (TDR) registry parameters in case NVidia Graphics Driver crashes +/- freezes unexpectedly:
http://docs.microsoft.com/windows-hardware/drivers/display/tdr-registry-keys/
http://www.reddit.com/r/battlefield_4/comments/1xzzn4/
http://answers.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/forum/all/registry-fix-for-videotimeoutdetectionandrecovery/deea25d5-d94a-47f8-a09f-be7ce56d5084/
http://www.pugetsystems.com/labs/hpc/Working-around-TDR-in-Windows-for-a-better-GPU-computing-experience-777/
http://github.com/MicrosoftDocs/windows-driver-docs/issues/1382/
http://developer.download.nvidia.com/NsightVisualStudio/2.2/Documentation/UserGuide/HTML/Content/Timeout_Detection_Recovery.htm
http://forum.giga-byte.co.uk/index.php?topic=4547.0
http://www.windowsphoneinfo.com/threads/i-modified-some-registry-keys-to-make-graphics-card-optimization-without-hanging-on.153714/
1st Things 1st:
***************
Make sure you have already upgraded to the current/newest version of the certified/official [not beta!] NVidia Graphics Driver
supported by your NVidia graphics/video card/controller/GPU model/(sub)type and your installed Windows NTx operating system(s)
[OS(es)] build(s), edition(s) + bit strength [32-bit (x86) +/- 64-bit (x64)]:
http://www.nvidia.com/download/find.aspx
http://www.nvidia.com/download/index.aspx
Only after that...
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\GraphicsDrivers]
"TdrLevel"=dword:0
"TdrDdiDelay"=dword:3c
"TdrDebugMode"=dword:3
"TdrDelay"=dword:3c
"TdrLimitTime"=dword:3c
"TdrLimitCount"=dword:3c
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\GraphicsDrivers\BasicDisplay]
"BasicDisplayUserNotified"=dword:0
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\GraphicsDrivers\DCI]
"Timeout"=dword:3c
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\GraphicsDrivers\TdrWatch]
"TDR_RECOVERY"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Control\GraphicsDrivers]
"TdrLevel"=dword:0
"TdrDdiDelay"=dword:3c
"TdrDebugMode"=dword:3
"TdrDelay"=dword:3c
"TdrLimitTime"=dword:3c
"TdrLimitCount"=dword:3c
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Control\GraphicsDrivers\BasicDisplay]
"BasicDisplayUserNotified"=dword:0
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Control\GraphicsDrivers\DCI]
"Timeout"=dword:3c
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Control\GraphicsDrivers\TdrWatch]
"TDR_RECOVERY"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Control\GraphicsDrivers]
"TdrLevel"=dword:0
"TdrDdiDelay"=dword:3c
"TdrDebugMode"=dword:3
"TdrDelay"=dword:3c
"TdrLimitTime"=dword:3c
"TdrLimitCount"=dword:3c
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Control\GraphicsDrivers\BasicDisplay]
"BasicDisplayUserNotified"=dword:0
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Control\GraphicsDrivers\DCI]
"Timeout"=dword:3c
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Control\GraphicsDrivers\TdrWatch]
"TDR_RECOVERY"=dword:1
;
------End cut & paste here------

* Turn OFF Aero Snap [align (all) open window(s) with screen margins] + Aero Shake [minimize (all) open window(s)] Desktop
features in Windows 7/8/8.1/10:
http://www.winaero.com/enable-or-disable-aero-shake-in-windows-10-with-these-methods/
http://www.winaero.com/disable-aero-snap-windows-10/

1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.

-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Explorer\Advanced]
"DisallowShaking"=dword:1
[HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Explorer\Advanced]
"DisallowShaking"=dword:1
[HKEY_USERS\.DEFAULT\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Explorer\Advanced]
"DisallowShaking"=dword:1
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Policies\Microsoft\Windows\Explorer]
"NoWindowMinimizingShortcuts"=dword:1
[HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Policies\Microsoft\Windows\Explorer]
"NoWindowMinimizingShortcuts"=dword:1
[HKEY_USERS\.DEFAULT\Software\Policies\Microsoft\Windows\Explorer]
"NoWindowMinimizingShortcuts"=dword:1
[HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Control Panel\Desktop]
"DockMoving"="0"
"WindowArrangementActive"="0"
[HKEY_USERS\.DEFAULT\Control Panel\Desktop]
"DockMoving"="0"
"WindowArrangementActive"="0"
;
------End cut & paste here------

* Turn OFF Online Tips and Help for Windows Settings (WS) a.k.a. Immersive Control Panel (ICP) a.k.a. native Control Panel
in Windows 10:
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/99351-enable-disable-online-tips-help-settings-app-windows-10-a.html
http://www.ghacks.net/2018/01/22/disable-online-tips-and-videos-in-the-windows-10-settings-app/
http://admx.help/?Category=Windows_10_2016&Policy=Microsoft.Policies.ControlPanel::AllowOnlineTips
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.

"AllowOnlineTips"=dword:0
;

* Turn ON Balloon/Info/Popup Tips, Taskbar Badges for buttons/icons, Taskbar Large Icons, Taskbar Animations, Hidden +
SuperHidden files/folders in Explorer/similar tools, Hidden File Extensions (*.ext) + turn OFF Aero Shake/Shaking to
prevent inadvertent/unexpected minimizing of open window(s) in Windows 7/8/8.1/10:
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/48186-taskbar-buttons-hide-show-badges-windows-10-a.html
http://www.groovypost.com/howto/windows-8-7-disable-notification-balloons-taskbar/
http://www.howtogeek.com/howto/windows-vista/disable-all-notification-balloons-in-windows-vista/
http://www.heelpbook.net/2019/windows-10-disable-notifications-and-notifications-balloons/
http://www.technorms.com/24581/

http://winaero.com/enable-or-disable-aero-shake-in-windows-10-with-these-methods/
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/62842-hide-show-file-name-extensions-windows-10-a.html
http://www.howtogeek.com/howto/windows-7/disable-aero-shake-in-windows-7/
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Explorer\Advanced]
"DisallowShaking"=dword:1
"EnableBalloonTips"=dword:1
"IconsOnly"=dword:0
"ShowSuperHidden"=dword:1
"Hidden"=dword:1
"HideFileExt"=dword:0
"ShowInfoTip"=dword:1
"SuperHidden"=dword:1
"StartButtonBalloonTip"=dword:2
"TaskbarAnimations"=dword:1
"TaskbarBadges"=dword:1
"TaskbarSmallIcons"=dword:0
[HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Explorer\Advanced]
"DisallowShaking"=dword:1
"EnableBalloonTips"=dword:1
"IconsOnly"=dword:0
"ShowSuperHidden"=dword:1
"Hidden"=dword:1
"HideFileExt"=dword:0
"ShowInfoTip"=dword:1
"SuperHidden"=dword:1
"StartButtonBalloonTip"=dword:2
"TaskbarAnimations"=dword:1
"TaskbarBadges"=dword:1
"TaskbarSmallIcons"=dword:0
[HKEY_USERS\.DEFAULT\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Explorer\Advanced]
"DisallowShaking"=dword:1
"EnableBalloonTips"=dword:1
"IconsOnly"=dword:0
"ShowSuperHidden"=dword:1
"Hidden"=dword:1
"HideFileExt"=dword:0
"ShowInfoTip"=dword:1
"SuperHidden"=dword:1
"StartButtonBalloonTip"=dword:2
"TaskbarAnimations"=dword:1
"TaskbarBadges"=dword:1
"TaskbarSmallIcons"=dword:0
;
------End cut & paste here------

* Turn OFF Clipboard Experience, Sync + certain annoying Clipboard Warnings in Windows 10:
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/110048-enable-disable-clipboard-sync-across-devices-windows-10-a.html
http://pureinfotech.com/disable-clipboard-windows-10/
http://pureinfotech.com/sync-clipboard-across-devices-windows-10/
http://www.winaero.com/enable-disable-clipboard-history-windows-10/
Access Clipboard settings: Run... [hold WinKey + press R] -> type this command:
ms-settings:clipboard
-> press Enter -> Sync across devices [must be logged/signed in with Microsoft Azure/Bing/Hotmail/Live/MSN/Outlook/Windows
Mail/WIP e-mail/membership/subscription account!] -> check "Never automatically sync text that I copy" box -> turn OFF
"Sync across devices" toggle switch.
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Policies\Microsoft\Windows\System]
"AllowCrossDeviceClipboard"=dword:0
;
------End cut & paste here------
NOTE:
These settings do NOT apply to Microsoft/3rd party Office/Excel/Outlook/other apps/programs!

* Turn ON Developer Mode to allow to install/use all signed Universal Windows Platforms (UWP) apps from all sources in Windows 10:
http://www.tenforums.com/tutorials/30136-turn-off-developer-mode-windows-10-a.html
http://techcult.com/enable-or-disable-developer-mode-in-windows-10/

http://admx.help/?Category=Windows_10_2016&Policy=Microsoft.Policies.Appx::AllowDevelopmentWithoutDevLicense
http://docs.microsoft.com/windows/apps/get-started/developer-mode-features-and-debugging/
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).

REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Policies\Microsoft\Windows\Appx]
"AllowAllTrustedApps"=dword:1

"AllowDevelopmentWithoutDevLicense"=dword:1
;
------End cut & paste here------

* Turn OFF Background Activity Moderator (BAM) [%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Drivers\bam.sys] + Desktop Activity Moderator (DAM)
[%WinDir%\SYSTEM32\Drivers\dam.sys] monitor drivers, especially if not using a laptop/notebook/portable, and don't need
to save battery power in Windows 10:
http://www.cellebrite.com/en/analyzing-program-execution-windows-artifacts/
http://www.andreafortuna.org/2018/05/23/forensic-artifacts-evidences-of-program-execution-on-windows-systems/
http://batcmd.com/windows/10/services/bam/
http://www.crowdstrike.com/blog/how-to-employ-featureusage-for-windows-10-taskbar-forensics/
http://docs.microsoft.com/windows/compatibility/desktop-activity-moderator/
http://batcmd.com/windows/10/services/dam/
Disable these 2 drivers (running as services) from a DOS console (command prompt) -> right-click CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE ->
Run as Administrator -> run these commands -> press Enter after each line:
ECHO Y|NET.EXE STOP bam
SC.EXE CONFIG bam START= disabled
ECHO Y|NET.EXE STOP dam
SC.EXE CONFIG dam START= disabled
OR:
1. Use Notepad or similar/better free(ware) plain text/ASCII editor:
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#TXT
to create a plain text Registry file containing the lines between Cut & Paste delimiters below.
2. Save it as plain text/ASCII file (Encode -> ANSI) with the REG extension (.REG).
3. Name it whatever you wish.
4. Right-click newly created .REG file.
5. Run as Administrator.
6. Answer Yes/OK to all prompts to register its information into your Registry.
-----Begin cut & paste here-----
REGEDIT4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\bam]
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\bam]
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\bam]
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\dam]
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\dam]
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\dam]
"Start"=dword:4
;
------End cut & paste here------
Restart (reboot) Windows for these changes to take effect.

* Turn OFF Application Virtualization (App-V) service + drivers in Windows 10 if not using any virtual deployed/streaming
client apps +/- cloud/server apps in a networked environment:
http://docs.microsoft.com/windows/application-management/app-v/appv-for-windows/

http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microsoft_App-V
Disable AppVClient service and these 3 App-V drivers (running as services) from a DOS console (command prompt) -> right-click
CMD shortcut/CMD.EXE -> Run as Administrator -> run these commands -> press Enter after each line:
ECHO Y|NET.EXE STOP AppVClient
SC.EXE CONFIG AppVClient START= disabled

SC.EXE CONFIG AppvStrm START= disabled
ECHO Y|NET.EXE STOP AppvVemgr

ECHO Y|NET.EXE STOP AppvVfs
SC.EXE CONFIG AppvVfs START= disabled
OR:

[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\AppVClient\Security]

"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:4

[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\AppVClient]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:4
[-HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\AppVClient\Security]
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\AppVClient]
"LaunchProtected"=dword:0
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\AppvStrm]
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\AppvStrm]
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\AppvStrm]
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\AppvVemgr]
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\AppvVemgr]
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet002\Services\AppvVemgr]
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\AppvVfs]
"Start"=dword:4
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\ControlSet001\Services\AppvVfs]
"Start"=dword:4

* Remove/Uninstall Windows 10 built-in/store Universal Windows Platforms (UWP) apps:
http://www.addictivetips.com/windows-tips/remove-default-windows-10-apps-using-powershell/
Uninstall all UWP apps for all users (example): right-click PowerShell shortcut or C:\WINDOWS\System32\WindowsPowerShell\v1.0\PowerShell.exe
[default location] -> Run as Administrator -> run this command -> press Enter:
Get-AppXPackage -AllUsers | Remove-AppXPackage

* Restore/Reinstall manually Windows Store app + Windows 10 built-in Universal Windows Platforms (UWP) apps:
http://www.winhelponline.com/blog/restore-windows-store-windows-10-uninstall-with-powershell/
Right-click PowerShell shortcut or C:\WINDOWS\System32\WindowsPowerShell\v1.0\PowerShell.exe [default location] -> Run as
Administrator -> run this command -> press Enter:
Get-AppXPackage -AllUsers Microsoft.WindowsStore | Foreach {Add-AppXPackage -DisableDevelopmentMode -Register "$($_.InstallLocation)\AppXManifest.xml"}
Windows Store app Uniform Resource Identifier (URI):
http://www.microsoft.com/p/microsoft-store/9wzdncrfjbmp/
Windows Store app product identification (ID) URI:
ms-windows-store://pdp?productId=9wzdncrfjbmp
Paste Windows Store app URI and/or desired UWP app URI
http://www.microsoft.com/p/microsoft-store/xxxxxxxxxxxxxx
or product identification ID URI
ms-windows-store://pdp?productId=xxxxxxxxxxxxxx
in the search box at this web site:
http://store.rg-adguard.net/
to download all required app components listed for your specific Windows 10 edition, build + bit strength -> (double-)click *.appx
and/or *.appxbundle file(s) to (re)install desired Windows Store/UWP app(s) -> log back into or restart Windows if prompted to do
so. You can also extract the entire contents of any downloaded *.appx/*.appxbundle archive using an unZIPping/unARChiving/unRARing
tool [free(ware)]
http://www.mdgx.com/toy.htm#ZIP
anywhere on your local storage drives/partitions/volumes, and copy file(s) necessary for proper function of selected app(s) to
desired location(s).
